KillMob = function(r0_207, r1_207)
  -- line: [0, 0] id: 207
  pcall(function()

    thismob = DetectMob2(r0_207)

      while true do
        task.wait()
        Buso()
        EquipWeapon()
        Tween23(thismob.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 15, 0))
        BringPos = thismob.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
        BringMob(r0_207)
        NoClip = true
        if thismob.Parent then
          local r0 = thismob:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
          if r0 then
            r0 = thismob:FindFirstChild("Humanoid").Health
            if r0 > 0 then
              r0 = thismob:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
              if r0 then
                r0 = r1_207()
                if r0 then
                  break
                end
              else
                break
              end
            else
              break
            end
          else
            break
          end
        else
          break
        end
      end
      NoClip = false
      CancelTween23()
    end
  end)
end

      return 
    end
    return 
  end
end

  while task.wait() do
    local r0 = _G.AutoKillV4
    if r0 then
      pcall(function()
        -- line: [0, 0] id: 430
        for r3, r4 in pairs(game.Workspace.Characters:GetChildren()) do
          if r4.Name ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Name and r4:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and r4:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and 0 < r4.Humanoid.Health and r4.Parent and (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - r4.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 230 then
            while true do
              task.wait()
              AutoHaki()
              EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)
              topos(r4.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(1, 1, 2))
              r4.HumanoidRootPart.Size = Vector3.new(60, 60, 60)
              r4.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false
              r4.Head.CanCollide = false
              r4.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0
              sethiddenproperty(game.Players.LocalPlayer, "SimulationRadius", math.huge)
              if _G.AutoKillV4 then
                local r5 = r4.Humanoid.Health
                if r5 > 0 then
                  r5 = r4.Parent
                  if r5 then
                    r5 = r4:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if r5 then
                      r5 = r4:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
                      if not r5 then
                        break
                      end
                    else
                      break
                    end
                  else
                    break
                  end
                else
                  break
                end
              else
                break
              end
            end
          end
        end
      end)
    end
  end
end)

r100_0 = function(r0)
  -- line: [0, 0] id: 610
  if workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Island " .. r0) then
    local r1 = 4500
    for r5, r6 in pairs(workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:GetChildren()) do
      if r6.Name == "Island " .. r0 and (r6.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < r1 then
        r1 = (r6.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
      end
    end
    for r5, r6 in pairs(workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:GetChildren()) do
      if r6.Name == "Island " .. r0 and (r6.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= r1 then
        return r6
      end
    end
  end
end

  }) do

      r5 = (r100_0(r4).Position - r6).Magnitude
      if r5 <= 4500 then
        return r100_0(r4)
      end
    end
  end
end
local r102_0 = function()
  -- line: [0, 0] id: 145
  local r0 = {}
  for r4, r5 in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
    if r5:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and r5:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and 0 < r5.Humanoid.Health and (r5.HumanoidRootPart.Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 1000 then
      table.insert(r0, r5)
    end
  end
  for r4, r5 in pairs(r0) do
    while true do
      task.wait(0.1)
      if r5:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
        local r6 = r5.Humanoid.Health
        if r6 > 0 then
          EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon)
          topos(r5.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0))
        end
      end
      local r6 = r5:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")
      if r6 then
        r6 = r5.Humanoid.Health
        if r6 <= 0 then
          break
        end
      else
        break
      end
    end
  end
end

          r4.Head.CanCollide = false

            r4.Humanoid.Animator:Destroy()

end)

  -- line: [0, 0] id: 583
  local r0 = next

  for r3, r4 in r0, r1, r2 do
    if typeof(r4) == "function" and getfenv(r4).script == game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Dodge") then
      local r5 = next
      local r6, r7 = getupvalues(r4)
      for r8, r9 in r5, r6, r7 do
        if tostring(r9) == "0.4" then
          setupvalue(r4, r8, 0)
        end
      end
    end
  end
end
